The detective only wanted the dry facts of the events.

澄清自己的意思

In such cases, their function is to provide factual information to clarify points raised and not to carry argument.
在这种情况下，他们的任务是提供事实依据来澄清观点，而不是继续辩论。
to clear the air
澄清事实
to set {or} put the record straight
澄清事实
to put sth straight
澄清某事

这种苹果汁是经传统工艺加工澄清的。

医生澄清说，他采用的诊断方法是无害的。
She clarified the butter in a small pan.

He could not be vindicated by any other principles.
Tā bù kěnéng yǐ rènhé qítā lǐyóu dédào chéngqīng。
他不可能以任何其他理由得到澄清。
Their theory is quite ambiguous, they should fight the case out and clarify the issues.

他们的理论相当模棱两可，他们应该澄清这些问题。
It is time to put the record straight and emphasise the quality of our management and the quality of our products.

现在是澄清问题，强调管理和产品的质量的的时候了。
To set the record straight, I was there to explain our position to the audience.
Wèile chéngqīng wùhuì，wǒ qù nà xiàng guānzhòng jiěshìle wǒmen de lìchǎng。

The group called a meeting to finally clear the air.

这个团体为了最后澄清事实而召开了一次会议。

wǎngfèi gōngfu

我们决不冤枉一个好人，也决不放过一个坏人。

We will never wrong a single good person nor let off a single bad one.

Tā dài zhe kūqiāngshuō biérén yuānwangtā le。

wǎngshā wúgū

wǎnghuó le bànbèizi

枉费工夫
wǎngfèi gōngfu 
waste time and energy
既然他不讲理，跟他争辩也是枉然。
Jìrán tā bù jiǎnɡlǐ, ɡēn tā zhēnɡbiàn yě shì wǎnɡrán。 
It\'s no use arguing with him when he refuses to listen to reason.
枉死鬼
wǎnɡsǐɡuǐ 
wronged souls
枉自讨论了那么多次，问题还是没解决。
Wǎngzì tǎolùn le nàme duō cì，wèntí háishi méi jiějué。
We have discussed the problem several times but to no purpose.
我是冤枉的。
Wǒ shì yuānwang de。
I was wrongly accused. or I am innocent.
冤枉好人
yuānwanghǎorén 
wrong an innocent person
在这件小事上，花那么多时间，真冤枉。
Zài zhèjiàn xiǎoshì shàng，huā nàme duō shíjiān，zhēn yuānwang。

矫枉过正
jiǎowǎngguòzhèng

枉法
wǎngfǎ
pervert (or bend) the law
他业绩这么好，也不枉你对他的培养。
Tā yèjì zhème hǎo，yě bùwǎng nǐ duì tā de péiyǎng。
His outstanding performance makes him worthy of your cultivation.
他在蚕室里一直喊着冤枉。
Tā zài cánshì lǐ yìzhí hǎn zhe yuānwang。

他这次获罪明显是被冤枉的。
Tā zhècì huòzuì míngxiǎn shì bèi yuānwǎng de。
It\'s obvious that his conviction was unjust.

You\'d better provide your evidence and not accuse an innocent person groundlessly.
事情不是你想象的那样，你不要屈枉我！
Shìqíng búshì nǐ xiǎng xiàng de nàyàng，nǐ búyào qūwǎng wǒ！
Things aren\'t like that, don\'t treat me unfairly.
他在“四清”运动中受到了迫害，是被冤枉的。
Tā zài“sìqīng”yùndòng zhōng shòudào le pòhài，shì bèi yuānwǎng de。
He was unfairly persecuted in the &quot;Four Clearances&quot;, which meant clearing of politics, clearing of organization, clearing of economy and clearing of ideology.
我们决不能姑息贪赃枉法的行为！
Wǒmen jué bùnéng gūxī tānzhāng wǎngfǎ de xíngwéi！
We must never tolerate any taking bribes and perverting justice.
感谢你能来枉顾小店，小弟真是三生有幸！
Gǎnxiè nǐ néng lái wǎnggù xiǎodiàn，xiǎodì zhēnshì sānshēng yǒuxìng！
Thank you for visiting my shop, it makes me feel very honored!
认识您真是前世的缘份，希望您以后能经常枉驾寒舍！
Rènshí nín zhēnshì qiánshì de yuánfèn，xīwàng nín yǐhòu néng jīngcháng wǎngjià hánshè！
It\'s our fate in our past lives that has brought us together. I hope that you can often visit my little house!
不要诬枉好人，否则你会遭到报应的。
Búyào wūwǎng hǎorén，fǒuzé nǐ huì zāodào bàoyìng de。
Do not calumniate good people, otherwise you will be punished.
根据他的所作所为，称呼他为乡愿一点都不冤枉。
Gēnjù tā de suǒzuò suǒwéi，chēnghū tā wéi xiāngyuàn yìdiǎn dōu bùyuānwang。
It is no exaggeration to call him a hypocrite, after what he has done.
因为不愿下车问路，他们跑了不少冤枉路。

你不要再枉费心机了，不属于你的东西终究是得不到的。
Nǐ búyào zài wǎngfèi xīnjīle，bù shǔyú nǐ de dōngxi zhōngjiū shì débúdào de。
Stop wasting your time and spirit. You can\'t get what does not belong to you.

Nà hóuzi de guài yàngzhēn kělè。
The monkey\'s antics are really amusing.
猴子性喜攀缘。
Hóuzi xìngxǐ pānyuán。
Monkeys have a natural inclination for climbing.
话说五百年前，有只大闹天宫的猴子被压在这里。
Huàshuō wǔbǎi niánqián，yǒu zhī dànào tiāngōng de hóuzi bèi yāzài zhèlǐ。
The story goes like this: 500 years ago, a monkey who  made big trouble in the heavenly palace was pressed under the mountain here.
猴山上猴子们欢闹玩耍，吸引不少游客的目光。
Hóushān shàng hóuzimen huānnào wánshuǎ，xīyǐn bùshǎo yóukè de mùguāng。
On the Monkey Mountain the monkeys frolicked and played happily, which attracted the eyes of many tourists.
猴子们经常互相搔痒。
Hóuzimen jīngcháng hùxiāng sāoyǎng。
Monkeys often titillate each other.
这些猴子的主要食物就是山上野生的各类山果。

The main food for these monkeys is wild mountain fruit.
这只猴子在树间上蹿下跳的，异常活跃。

The monkey is jumping up and down in the trees and is extremely enthusiastic.
他从小就嘴刁，所以营养不良，瘦得像个猴子。

猴子的动作非常敏捷。
Hóuzǐ de dòngzuò fēicháng mǐnjié.
Monkeys are extremely agile.
这小子猴儿精的。
Zhè xiǎozi hóurjīng de。
That fellow is awfully shrewd.
这孩子是个猴儿精。

The boy is a mischief-maker.

广(狭)义相对论
guǎng（xiá）yì xiāngduìlùn
the general (special) theory of relativity
狭义。
广义的现代汉语包括普通话和方言，狭义的现代汉语只指普通话
&quot;金&quot;广义指一切金属，狭义则专指黄金。
special (或 restricted) theory of relativity
狭义相对论
in the narrow sense of the word
